
if exists (select 1
   from sys.sysreferences r join sys.sysobjects o on (o.id = r.constid and o.type = 'F')
   where r.fkeyid = object_id('ActivityLog') and o.name = 'FK_ACTIVITY_REFERENCE_USER')
alter table ActivityLog
   drop constraint FK_ACTIVITY_REFERENCE_USER
go

/*==============================================================*/
/* Table: ActivityLog                                           */
/*==============================================================*/
create table ActivityLog (
   Id                   int                  identity,
   UserId               int                  null,
   LogDate              datetime             not null default getdate(),
   Activity             nvarchar(255)        not null,
   Result               nvarchar(255)        null,
   IpAddress            nvarchar(50)         null,
   CreatedOn            datetime2            not null default getdate(),
   CreatedBy            int                  null,
   ChangedOn            datetime2            not null default getdate(),
   ChangedBy            int                  null,
   constraint PK_ACTIVITYLOG primary key (Id)
)
go

/*==============================================================*/
/* Index: IndexActivityLogUserId                                */
/*==============================================================*/
create index IndexActivityLogUserId on ActivityLog (
UserId ASC
)
go

/*==============================================================*/
/* Index: IndexActivityLogLogDate                               */
/*==============================================================*/
create index IndexActivityLogLogDate on ActivityLog (
LogDate ASC
)
go

/*==============================================================*/
/* Table: Class                                                 */
/*==============================================================*/
create table Class (
   Id                   int                  identity,
   ClassNumber          nvarchar(30)         not null default 'New Class',
   CourseId             int                  not null,
   Course               nvarchar(75)         null,
   Location             nvarchar(50)         not null,
   StartDate            date                 not null,
   EndDate              date                 not null,
   MaxEnrollments       int                  not null,
   TotalEnrollments     int                  not null default 0,
   CreatedOn            datetime2            not null default getdate(),

   add constraint FK_VIEWED_REFERENCE_USER foreign key (UserId)
      references "User" (Id)

   add constraint FK_ACTIVITY_REFERENCE_USER foreign key (UserId)
      references "User" (Id)

      references Course (Id)

      references Department (Id)

      references Instructor (Id)

   add constraint FK_DATALOG_REFERENCE_USER foreign key (UserId)
      references "User" (Id)

   add constraint FK_ENROLLME_REFERENCE_STUDENT foreign key (StudentId)
      references Student (Id)
go

   add constraint FK_ENROLLME_REFERENCE_CLASS foreign key (ClassId)
      references Class (Id)
go

   add constraint FK_ERROR_REFERENCE_USER foreign key (UserId)
      references "User" (Id)

alter table History
   add constraint FK_HISTORY_REFERENCE_USER foreign key (UserId)
      references "User" (Id)
go

   add constraint FK_PREFEREN_REFERENCE_USER foreign key (UserId)
      references "User" (Id)
go

alter table Quiz
   add constraint FK_QUIZ_REFERENCE_ENROLLME foreign key (EnrollmentId)
      references Enrollment (Id)
go

   add constraint FK_STUDENT_REFERENCE_COUNTRY foreign key (CountryId)
      references Country (Id)
go

   add constraint FK_VIEWFILT_REFERENCE_VIEW foreign key (ViewId)
      references "View" (Id)

   add constraint FK_VIEWSORT_REF2_VIEW foreign key (ViewId)
      references "View" (Id)

   add constraint FK_VIEWSORT_REF1_VIEW foreign key (ViewId)
      references "View" (Id)
